padding-left: 0.289em;">25500</span><span class="mtext" id="MathJax-Span-194" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">&nbsp;</span><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-195" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">p</span><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-196" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">p</span><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-197" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">m</span></span><span style="display: inline-block; <p>[হাজারী স্যার: সংস্করণ-২০২২, পৃষ্ঠা-৪৩২]</p>

position: relative; width: 3.363em; height: 0px; margin-right: 0.125em; margin-left: 0.125em;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(3.445em, 1003.2em, 4.141em, -999.998em); top: -4.424em; left: 50%; margin-left: -1.596em;"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-253"><span class="mn" id="MathJax-Span-254" style="font-size: 70.7%; font-family: MathJax_Main;">1000</span><span class="mo" id="MathJax-Span-255" style="font-size: 70.7%; font-family: MathJax_Main;">×</span><span class="mn" id="MathJax-Span-256" style="font-size: 70.7%; font-family: MathJax_Main;">10.6</span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.018em;"></span></span><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(3.445em, 1002.62em, 4.141em, -999.998em); top: -3.645em; left: 50%; margin-left: -1.35em;"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-257"><span class="mn" id="MathJax-Span-258" style="font-size: 70.7%; font-family: MathJax_Main;">106</span><span class="mo" id="MathJax-Span-259" style="font-size: 70.7%; font-family: MathJax_Main;">×</span><span class="mn" id="MathJax-Span-260" style="font-size: 70.7%; font-family: MathJax_Main;">250</span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.018em;"></span></span><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(0.904em, 1003.36em, 1.191em, -999.998em); top: -1.268em; left: 0em;"><span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; vertical-align: 0em; border-top: 1.5px solid; width: 3.363em; height: 0px;"></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 1.068em;"></span></span></span></span><span class="mo" id="MathJax-Span-261" style="font-family: MathJax_Main; padding-left: 0.289em;">=</span><span class="mn" id="MathJax-Span-262" style="font-family: MathJax_Main; padding-left: 0.289em;">0.4</span><span class="mtext" id="MathJax-Span-263" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">&nbsp;</span><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-264" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">M</span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 1.969em;"></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; vertical-align: -0.497em; border-left: 0px solid; width: 0px; height: 1.652em;"></span></span></nobr><span class="MJX_Assistive_MathML" role="presentation"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><mi mathvariant="normal">S</mi><mo>=</mo><mfrac><mrow><mn>1000</mn><mtext>&nbsp;</mtext><mi mathvariant="normal">W</mi></mrow><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">M</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">V</mi></mrow></mfrac><mo>=</mo><mfrac><mrow><mn>1000</mn><mo>×</mo><mn>10.6</mn></mrow><mrow><mn>106</mn><mo>×</mo><mn>250</mn></mrow></mfrac><mo>=</mo><mn>0.4</mn><mtext>&nbsp;</mtext><mi mathvariant="normal">M</mi></math></span></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-25">\rm S=\frac{1000\ W}{MV}=\frac{1000\times10.6}{106\times250}=0.4\ M</script></span></p>

<p>[হাজারী স্যার: সংস্করণ-২০২২, পৃষ্ঠা- ৪২৫]</p>

                                            <p>আয়োডোমিতিক টাইট্রেশনের মাধ্যমে কোনো দ্রবণে কোন আয়নের পরিমাণ নির্ণয় করা হয়?</p>

width: 0px; height: 1.969em;"></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; vertical-align: -0.497em; border-left: 0px solid; width: 0px; height: 2.052em;"></span></span></nobr><span class="MJX_Assistive_MathML" role="presentation"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><msub><mi mathvariant="normal">E</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">k</mi></msub><mo>=</mo><mfrac><msup><mi mathvariant="normal">P</mi><mn>2</mn></msup><mrow><mn>2</mn><mi mathvariant="normal">m</mi></mrow></mfrac><mo>=</mo><mfrac><msup><mrow><mo>(</mo><mn>200</mn><mo>)</mo></mrow><mn>2</mn></msup><mrow><mn>2</mn><mo>×</mo><mn>2000</mn></mrow></mfrac><mo>=</mo><mn>10</mn><mtext>&nbsp;</mtext><mi mathvariant="normal">J</mi></math></span></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-76">\rm E_k=\frac{P^2}{2m}=\frac{\left(200\right)^2}{2\times2000}=10\ J </script></span></p>

<p>[ইসহাক স্যার: সংস্করণ- ২০২২, পৃষ্ঠা- ৩৫৩]</p>
</span>
                                    </div>

                                        <span style="color: black !important; font-weight: bold;">Solution:</span>
                                        <br>
                                        <span style="color: black !important;"><p><span class="math-tex"><span class="MathJax_Preview" style="color: inherit; display: none;"></span><span class="MathJax" id="MathJax-Element-81-Frame" tabindex="0" style="position: relative;" data-mathml="<math xmlns=&quot;http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML&quot;><mi mathvariant=&quot;normal&quot;>E</mi><mo>=</mo><mfrac><msup><mi mathvariant=&quot;normal&quot;>P</mi><mn>2</mn></msup><mrow><mn>2</mn><mi mathvariant=&quot;normal&quot;>m</mi></mrow></mfrac><mo stretchy=&quot;false&quot;>&amp;#x21D2;</mo><msup><mi mathvariant=&quot;normal&quot;>P</mi><mn>2</mn></msup><mo>=</mo><mn>2</mn><mi mathvariant=&quot;normal&quot;>m</mi><mi mathvariant=&quot;normal&quot;>E</mi><mo>&amp;#x2234;</mo><mi mathvariant=&quot;normal&quot;>P</mi><mo>=</mo><msqrt><mn>2</mn><mi mathvariant=&quot;normal&quot;>m</mi><mi mathvariant=&quot;normal&quot;>E</mi></msqrt></math>" role="presentation"><nobr aria-hidden="true"><span class="math" id="MathJax-Span-873" style="width: 15.576em; display: inline-block;"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 12.748em; height: 0px; font-size: 122%;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(1.027em, 1012.75em, 2.666em, -999.998em); position: relative; width: 1.109em; height: 0px;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(3.199em, 1000.62em, 4.141em, -999.998em); top: -4.014em; left: 0em;"><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-886" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">P</span><span style="display: inline-block; padding-left: 0.289em;">=</span><span class="msqrt" id="MathJax-Span-895" style="padding-left: 0.289em;"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 2.871em; height: 0px;"><span style="position: absolute; width: 0px; height: 4.018em;"></span></span><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(3.609em, 1002.05em, 3.895em, -999.998em); top: -4.588em; left: 0.822em;"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; font-family: MathJax_Main; top: -4.014em; left: 1.355em;">−<span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.018em;"></span></span><span style="font-family: MathJax_Main; position: absolute; top: -4.014em; width: 0px; height: 4.018em;"></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.018em;"></span></span><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(3.076em, 1000.86em, 4.346em, -999.998em); width: 0px; height: 2.174em;"></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; vertical-align: -0.497em; border-left: 0px solid; width: 0px; height: 1.802em;"></span></span></nobr><span class="MJX_Assistive_MathML" role="presentation"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><mi mathvariant="normal">E</mi><mo>=</mo><mfrac><msup><mi mathvariant="normal">P</mi><mn>2</mn></msup><mrow><mn>2</mn><mi mathvariant="normal">m</mi></mrow></mfrac><mo stretchy="false">⇒</mo><msup><mi mathvariant="normal">P</mi><mn>2</mn></msup><mo>=</mo><mn>2</mn><mi mathvariant="normal">m</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">E</mi><mo>∴</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">P</mi><mo>=</mo><msqrt><mn>2</mn><mi mathvariant="normal">m</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">E</mi></msqrt></math></span></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-81">\rm E=\frac{P^2}{2m}\Rightarrow P^2=2mE\therefore P=\sqrt{2mE}</script></span></p>

<p>[ইসহাক স্যার: সংস্করণ- ২০২২, পৃষ্ঠা- ৩৫৩]</p>

                                <div class="col-md-12" style="padding-left:0px; padding-right:0px;">
                                    <div class="row">
                                        <div class="serial">
                                            <span>Question 69 </span>
                                        </div>
                                        <div class="questionText" style="display: block;">
                                            <p>পৃথিবীর গড় ঘনত্ব কত?</p>

</label>
                                                <span class="fas fa-check"></span>
                                            </div>
                                        </div>
                                    </div>
                                </div>
                                    <div class="row solveText" style="display: block; padding:10px; color:#077307; overflow-x: auto; background-color: #d7f7d4;">
                                        <span style="color: black !important; font-weight: bold;">Solution:</span>
                                        <br>
                                        <span style="color: black !important;"><p>জেনে রাখো: ফাঁপা গোলকের বাইরে এর কেন্দ্র হতে r দূরত্বে বিভব <span class="math-tex"><span class="MathJax_Preview" style="color: inherit;
